				SELECT 
					COUNT(*) AS totaal
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1 

				SELECT 
					MAX(LAATSTE_AANPASSING) AS LAATSTE_AANPASSING
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1 

				SELECT 
					*
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1  ORDER BY SORTEER_VOLGORDE, ID

				SELECT 
					COUNT(*) AS totaal
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1 

				SELECT 
					MAX(LAATSTE_AANPASSING) AS LAATSTE_AANPASSING
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1 

				SELECT 
					*
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1  ORDER BY ID 

				SELECT 
					COUNT(*) AS totaal
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1 

				SELECT 
					MAX(LAATSTE_AANPASSING) AS LAATSTE_AANPASSING
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1 

				SELECT 
					*
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1  ORDER BY ID DESC 

				SELECT 
					COUNT(*) AS totaal
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1 

				SELECT 
					MAX(LAATSTE_AANPASSING) AS LAATSTE_AANPASSING
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1 

				SELECT 
					*
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1  ORDER BY SORTEER_VOLGORDE, ID LIMIT 0 , 2 

				SELECT 
					COUNT(*) AS totaal
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1  AND GROEP=1

				SELECT 
					MAX(LAATSTE_AANPASSING) AS LAATSTE_AANPASSING
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1  AND GROEP=1

				SELECT 
					*
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1  AND GROEP=1 ORDER BY SORTEER_VOLGORDE, ID

				SELECT 
					COUNT(*) AS totaal
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1 

				SELECT 
					MAX(LAATSTE_AANPASSING) AS LAATSTE_AANPASSING
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1 

				SELECT 
					ID, OMSCHRIJVING
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1  ORDER BY SORTEER_VOLGORDE, ID LIMIT 0 , 2 

				SELECT 
					COUNT(*) AS totaal
				FROM
					`types_view`  WHERE 1=1
